        In 2010, <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Nick_Vernier_Band" title="Nick Vernier Band" id="mwA0g">Nick Vernier Band</a> created a digital "Monkees reunion" through the release of <i id="mwA0k"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Nick_Vernier_Band_Sessions_(album)" title="Nick Vernier Band Sessions (album)" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA0o">Mister Bob (featuring the Monkees)</a>,</i><sup about="#mwt637" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-132" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-132"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-132" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 131;" id="mwA0s"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA0w">[131]</span></a></sup> a new song produced under license from <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Rhino_Entertainment" title="Rhino Entertainment" id="mwA00">Rhino Entertainment</a>, containing vocal samples from the band's recording "Zilch".
        The <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Contract_bridge" title="Contract bridge" id="mwA04">contract bridge</a> <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Bridge_convention" title="Bridge convention" id="mwA08">convention</a> known as either <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Last_Train_(bridge)" title="Last Train (bridge)" id="mwA1A">Last Train</a> or Last Train to Clarksville was so named by its inventor, <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Jeff_Meckstroth" title="Jeff Meckstroth" id="mwA1E">Jeff Meckstroth</a>, after the Monkees' song.<sup about="#mwt642" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-133" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-133"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-133" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 132;" id="mwA1I"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA1M">[132]</span></a></sup></p>
        
        <section data-mw-section-id="30" id="mwA1Q"><h4 id="Comic_books">Comic books</h4>
        <p id="mwA1U">A comic book series, <i id="mwA1Y">The Monkees</i>, was published in the United States by <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Dell_Comics" title="Dell Comics" id="mwA1c">Dell Comics</a>, which ran for 17 issues from 1967 to 1969.<sup about="#mwt647" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-134" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-134"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-134" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 133;" id="mwA1g"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA1k">[133]</span></a></sup></p>
        
        <p id="mwA1o">In the United Kingdom, a <i id="mwA1s"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Daily_Mirror" title="Daily Mirror" id="mwA1w">Daily Mirror</a></i> "Crazy Cartoon Book" featured four comic stories as well as four photos of the Monkees, all in black and white; it was published in 1967.</p>
        
        </section><section data-mw-section-id="31" id="mwA10"><h4 id="Biopic">Biopic</h4>
        <p id="mwA14">In 2000, <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./VH-1" title="VH-1" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA18">VH-1</a> produced the television biopic <i id="mwA2A"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Daydream_Believers:_The_Monkees'_Story" title="Daydream Believers: The Monkees' Story" id="mwA2E">Daydream Believers: The Monkees' Story</a></i>.<sup about="#mwt652" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-135" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-135"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-135" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 134;" id="mwA2I"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA2M">[134]</span></a></sup> In 2002, the movie was released on DVD and featured both commentaries and interviews with Dolenz, Jones and Tork. The aired version did differ from the DVD release, as the TV version had an extended scene with all four Monkees meeting the Beatles, but with a shortened Cleveland concert segment. It was also available on VHS.</p>
        
        </section><section data-mw-section-id="32" id="mwA2Q"><h4 id="Musical">Musical</h4>
        <p id="mwA2U">A stage musical opened in the UK at the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Manchester_Opera_House" title="Manchester Opera House" id="mwA2Y">Manchester Opera House</a> on Friday March 30, 2012, and was dedicated to Davy Jones (the Jones family attended the official opening on April 3).<sup about="#mwt661" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-Playbill_136-0" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"Playbill"},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-Playbill-136"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-Playbill-136" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 135;" id="mwA2c"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA2g">[135]</span></a></sup> The production is a <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Jukebox_musical" title="Jukebox musical" id="mwA2k">Jukebox musical</a> and starred Stephen Kirwan, Ben Evans, Tom Parsons and Oliver Savile<sup about="#mwt662" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-Playbill_136-1" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"Playbill"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-Playbill-136" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 135;" id="mwA2o"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA2s">[135]</span></a></sup> as actors playing the parts of the Monkees (respectively Dolenz, Jones, Nesmith, Tork) who are hired by an unscrupulous businessman to go on a world tour pretending to be the real band. The show includes 18 Monkees songs plus numbers by other 60s artists. It ran in <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Manchester" title="Manchester" id="mwA2w">Manchester</a> as part of the "Manchester Gets it First" program until April 14, 2012, before a UK tour.<sup about="#mwt663" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-Playbill_136-2" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"Playbill"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-Playbill-136" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 135;" id="mwA20"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA24">[135]</span></a></sup><sup about="#mwt667" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-BBC_Musical_137-0" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"BBC Musical"},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-BBC_Musical-137"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-BBC_Musical-137" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 136;" id="mwA28"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA3A">[136]</span></a></sup> Following its Manchester run, the show appeared in the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Glasgow_King's_Theatre" title="Glasgow King's Theatre" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA3E">Glasgow King's Theatre</a> and the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Sunderland_Empire_Theatre" title="Sunderland Empire Theatre" id="mwA3I">Sunderland Empire Theatre</a>.<sup about="#mwt668" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-Playbill_136-3" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"Playbill"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-Playbill-136" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 135;" id="mwA3M"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA3Q">[135]</span></a></sup></p>
        
        </section></section></section><section data-mw-section-id="33" id="mwA3U"><h2 id="Awards_and_achievements">Awards and achievements</h2>
        <section data-mw-section-id="34" id="mwA3Y"><h3 id="Grammy_Awards">Grammy Awards</h3>
        <p id="mwA3c">The <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Grammy_Awards" title="Grammy Awards" id="mwA3g">Grammy Awards</a> is an accolade by the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./National_Academy_of_Recording_Arts_and_Sciences" title="National Academy of Recording Arts and Sciences" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA3k">National Academy of Recording Arts and Sciences</a> (NARAS) of the United States to recognize outstanding achievement in the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Music_industry" title="Music industry" id="mwA3o">music industry</a>. It shares recognition of the music industry as that of the other performance arts: <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Emmy_Award" title="Emmy Award" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA3s">Emmy Awards</a> (television), the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Tony_Award" title="Tony Award" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA3w">Tony Awards</a> (stage performance), and the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Academy_Award" title="Academy Award" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA30">Academy Awards</a> (motion pictures).</p>

        <th style="width:15%;" id="mwA4Q">Result</th></tr>

        <td id="mwA4g"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Grammy_Award_for_Best_Contemporary_Song" title="Grammy Award for Best Contemporary Song" id="mwA4k">Best Contemporary (R&amp;R) Recording</a></td>
        <td rowspan="2" id="mwA4o">"Last Train to Clarksville"</td>
        <td style="background: #FFE3E3; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center; " class="no table-no2 notheme" typeof="mw:Transclusion" about="#mwt669" data-mw='{"parts":["| ",{"template":{"target":{"wt":"nom","href":"./Template:Nom"},"params":{},"i":0}}]}' id="mwA4s">Nominated</td></tr>

        <td style="background: #FFE3E3; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center; " class="no table-no2 notheme" typeof="mw:Transclusion" about="#mwt670" data-mw='{"parts":["| ",{"template":{"target":{"wt":"nom","href":"./Template:Nom"},"params":{},"i":0}}]}' id="mwA48">Nominated</td></tr>

        <td rowspan="2" style="text-align:center;" id="mwA5E"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./10th_Annual_Grammy_Awards" title="10th Annual Grammy Awards" id="mwA5I">1968</a></td>
        <td id="mwA5M"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Best_Performance_by_a_Vocal_Group" title="Best Performance by a Vocal Group" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA5Q">Best Performance by a Vocal Group</a></td>
        <td rowspan="2" id="mwA5U">"I'm a Believer"</td>
        <td style="background: #FFE3E3; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center; " class="no table-no2 notheme" typeof="mw:Transclusion" about="#mwt671" data-mw='{"parts":["| ",{"template":{"target":{"wt":"nom","href":"./Template:Nom"},"params":{},"i":0}}]}' id="mwA5Y">Nominated</td></tr>
        <tr id="mwA5c">
        <td id="mwA5g"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Grammy_Award_for_Best_Pop_Performance_by_a_Duo_or_Group_with_Vocal" title="Grammy Award for Best Pop Performance by a Duo or Group with Vocal" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA5k">Best Contemporary Group Performance (Vocal or Instrumental)</a></td>
        <td style="background: #FFE3E3; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center; " class="no table-no2 notheme" typeof="mw:Transclusion" about="#mwt672" data-mw='{"parts":["| ",{"template":{"target":{"wt":"nom","href":"./Template:Nom"},"params":{},"i":0}}]}' id="mwA5o">Nominated</td></tr>
        </tbody></table>
        
        </section><section data-mw-section-id="35" id="mwA5s"><h3 id="Notable_achievements">Notable achievements</h3>
        <ul id="mwA5w"><li id="mwA50">Gave the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Jimi_Hendrix_Experience" title="Jimi Hendrix Experience" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA54">Jimi Hendrix Experience</a> their first U.S. concert tour exposure as an opening act in July 1967.<sup about="#mwt677" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-138" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-138"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-138" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 137;" id="mwA58"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA6A">[137]</span></a></sup> <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Jimi_Hendrix" title="Jimi Hendrix" id="mwA6E">Jimi Hendrix</a>'s heavy <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Psychedelic_rock" title="Psychedelic rock" id="mwA6I">psychedelic</a> guitar and sexual overtones did not go over well with the teenage girls in the audience, which eventually led to his leaving the tour early.</li>
        <li id="mwA6M">The band inspired <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Gene_Roddenberry" title="Gene Roddenberry" id="mwA6Q">Gene Roddenberry</a> to introduce the character of <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Pavel_Chekov" title="Pavel Chekov" id="mwA6U">Chekov</a> in his <i id="mwA6Y"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Star_Trek" title="Star Trek" id="mwA6c">Star Trek</a></i> TV series in response to the popularity of Davy Jones, complete with hairstyle and appearance mimicking that of Jones.<sup about="#mwt680" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-139" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-139"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-139" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 138;" id="mwA6g"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA6k">[138]</span></a></sup><sup about="#mwt681" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-140" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-140"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-140" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 139;" id="mwA6o"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA6s">[139]</span></a></sup></li>
        <li id="mwA6w">Inducted into America's Pop Music Hall of Fame in 2014.<sup about="#mwt687" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-141" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-141"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-141" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 140;" id="mwA60"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA64">[140]</span></a></sup><sup about="#mwt691" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-142" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-142"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-142" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 141;" id="mwA68"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA7A">[141]</span></a></sup></li>
        <li id="mwA7E">Honored by the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Music_Business_Association" title="Music Business Association" id="mwA7I">Music Business Association (Music Biz)</a> with an Outstanding Achievement Award celebrating the band's 50th anniversary on May 16, 2016.<sup about="#mwt696" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-143" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-143"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-143" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 142;" id="mwA7M"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA7Q">[142]</span></a></sup></li>
        <li id="mwA7U">Inducted into the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Vocal_Group_Hall_of_Fame" title="Vocal Group Hall of Fame" id="mwA7Y">Vocal Group Hall of Fame</a> in 2007.<sup about="#mwt701" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-144" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-144"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-144" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 143;" id="mwA7c"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA7g">[143]</span></a></sup></li></ul>
        
        </section></section><section data-mw-section-id="36" id="mwA7k"><h2 id="Controversies">Controversies</h2>
        <section data-mw-section-id="37" id="mwA7o"><h3 id="Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame">Rock and Roll Hall of Fame</h3>
        <p id="mwA7s">Various magazines and news outlets, such as <i id="mwA7w"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Time_(magazine)" title="Time (magazine)" id="mwA70">Time</a></i>,<sup about="#mwt714" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-145" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-145"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-145" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 144;" id="mwA74"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA78">[144]</span></a></sup> <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./NPR" title="NPR" id="mwA8A">NPR</a>,<sup about="#mwt718" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-146" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-146"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-146" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 145;" id="mwA8E"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA8I">[145]</span></a></sup> <i id="mwA8M"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./The_Christian_Science_Monitor" title="The Christian Science Monitor" id="mwA8Q">The Christian Science Monitor</a></i>,<sup about="#mwt722" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-CSM_147-0" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"CSM"},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-CSM-147"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-CSM-147" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 146;" id="mwA8U"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA8Y">[146]</span></a></sup> <i id="mwA8c"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Goldmine_(magazine)" title="Goldmine (magazine)" id="mwA8g">Goldmine</a></i>,<sup about="#mwt726" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-148" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-148"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-148" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 147;" id="mwA8k"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA8o">[147]</span></a></sup><sup about="#mwt730" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-149" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-149"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-149" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 148;" id="mwA8s"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA8w">[148]</span></a></sup> <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Yahoo!_Music" title="Yahoo! Music" id="mwA80">Yahoo! Music</a><sup about="#mwt734" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-150" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-150"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-150" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 149;" id="mwA84"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA88">[149]</span></a></sup> and <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./MSNBC" title="MSNBC" id="mwA9A">MSNBC</a><sup about="#mwt738" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-151" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-151"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-151" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 150;" id="mwA9E"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA9I">[150]</span></a></sup> have argued that the Monkees belong in the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame. In 1992, Davy Jones told <i id="mwA9M"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./People_(magazine)" title="People (magazine)" id="mwA9Q">People</a></i> that he knew the Monkees would never make the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame.<sup about="#mwt742" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-152" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-152"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-152" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 151;" id="mwA9U"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA9Y">[151]</span></a></sup> In June 2007, Peter Tork complained to the <i id="mwA9c"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./New_York_Post" title="New York Post" id="mwA9g">New York Post</a></i> that <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Jann_Wenner" title="Jann Wenner" id="mwA9k">Jann Wenner</a> had "<a rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/blackball" title="wiktionary:blackball" class="extiw" id="mwA9o">blackballed</a>" the Monkees from being inducted into the <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame" title="Rock and Roll Hall of Fame" id="mwA9s">Rock and Roll Hall of Fame</a>. Tork contended that Wenner held a grudge against the Monkees because the band members did not always write their own songs or play their own instruments during their early years.<sup about="#mwt743" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-CSM_147-1" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"CSM"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-CSM-147" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 146;" id="mwA9w"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwA90">[146]</span></a></sup></p>
        
        </section></section><section data-mw-section-id="38" id="mwA94"><h2 id="Members">Members</h2>
        <ul id="mwA98"><li id="mwA-A"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Micky_Dolenz" title="Micky Dolenz" id="mwA-E">Micky Dolenz</a><span typeof="mw:Entity" id="mwA-I"> </span>– lead and backing vocals, rhythm guitar, drums, percussion (1966–1971, 1976, 1986–1989, 1996–1997, 2001–2002, 2011–2021)</li>
        <li id="mwA-M"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Davy_Jones_(musician)" title="Davy Jones (musician)" id="mwA-Q">Davy Jones</a><span typeof="mw:Entity" id="mwA-U"> </span>– lead and backing vocals, percussion, drums, rhythm guitar, bass (1966–1971, 1976, 1986–1989, 1996–1997, 2001–2002, 2011–2012; his death)</li>
        <li id="mwA-Y"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Michael_Nesmith" title="Michael Nesmith" id="mwA-c">Michael Nesmith</a><span typeof="mw:Entity" id="mwA-g"> </span>– lead and rhythm guitars, keyboards, backing and lead vocals (1966–1970, 1986, 1989, 1996–1997, 2012–2014, 2016, 2018–2021; his death)</li>
        <li id="mwA-k"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Peter_Tork" title="Peter Tork" id="mwA-o">Peter Tork</a><span typeof="mw:Entity" id="mwA-s"> </span>– bass, rhythm and lead guitars, keyboards, banjo, backing and occasional lead vocals (1966–1968, 1976, 1986–1989, 1996–1997, 2001, 2011–2018; died 2019)</li></ul>

        </section></section><section data-mw-section-id="40" id="mwA-4"><h2 id="Discography">Discography</h2>
        <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" about="#mwt747" typeof="mw:Extension/templatestyles mw:Transclusion" data-mw='{"parts":[{"template":{"target":{"wt":"Main","href":"./Template:Main"},"params":{"1":{"wt":"The Monkees discography"}},"i":0}}]}' id="mwA-8"/><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" about="#mwt747" id="mwA_A">Main article: <a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./The_Monkees_discography" title="The Monkees discography">The Monkees discography</a></div>
        <ul id="mwA_E"><li id="mwA_I"><i id="mwA_M"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./The_Monkees_(album)" title="The Monkees (album)" id="mwA_Q">The Monkees</a></i> (1966)</li>
        <li id="mwA_U"><i id="mwA_Y"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./More_of_The_Monkees" title="More of The Monkees" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA_c">More of The Monkees</a></i> (1967)</li>
        <li id="mwA_g"><i id="mwA_k"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Headquarters_(the_Monkees_album)" title="Headquarters (the Monkees album)" class="mw-redirect" id="mwA_o">Headquarters</a></i> (1967)</li>
        <li id="mwA_s"><i id="mwA_w"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Pisces,_Aquarius,_Capricorn_&amp;_Jones_Ltd." title="Pisces, Aquarius, Capricorn &amp; Jones Ltd." id="mwA_0">Pisces, Aquarius, Capricorn &amp; Jones Ltd.</a></i> (1967)</li>
        <li id="mwA_4"><i id="mwA_8"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./The_Birds,_The_Bees_&amp;_the_Monkees" title="The Birds, The Bees &amp; the Monkees" class="mw-redirect" id="mwBAA">The Birds, The Bees &amp; the Monkees</a></i> (1968)</li>
        <li id="mwBAE"><i id="mwBAI"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Head_(The_Monkees_album)" title="Head (The Monkees album)" id="mwBAM">Head</a></i> (1968)</li>
        <li id="mwBAQ"><i id="mwBAU"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./Instant_Replay_(The_Monkees_album)" title="Instant Replay (The Monkees album)" id="mwBAY">Instant Replay</a></i> (1969)</li>
        <li id="mwBAc"><i id="mwBAg"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./The_Monkees_Present" title="The Monkees Present" id="mwBAk">The Monkees Present</a></i> (1969)</li>

        </section><section data-mw-section-id="41" id="mwBBk"><h2 id="Tours">Tours</h2>

        <li id="mwBCo">Justus Tour (1997)</li>
        <li id="mwBCs">North American Tour (1997) <small id="mwBCw">(Dolenz, Jones, Tork)</small></li>
        <li id="mwBC0">U.S. Tour (2001) <small id="mwBC4">(Dolenz, Jones, Tork; Tork removed from the tour partway through)</small></li>

        <li id="mwBDE"><a rel="mw:WikiLink" href="./An_Evening_with_The_Monkees:_The_45th_Anniversary_Tour" title="An Evening with The Monkees: The 45th Anniversary Tour" id="mwBDI">An Evening with The Monkees: The 45th Anniversary Tour</a> (2011) <small id="mwBDM">(Dolenz, Jones, Tork)</small></li>
        <li id="mwBDQ">An Evening with The Monkees (Fall 2012) <small id="mwBDU">(Dolenz, Nesmith, Tork)</small><sup about="#mwt754" class="mw-ref reference" id="cite_ref-rhino2012tour_101-1" rel="dc:references" typeof="mw:Extension/ref" data-mw='{"name":"ref","attrs":{"name":"rhino2012tour"},"body":{"id":"mw-reference-text-cite_note-rhino2012tour-101"}}'><a href="./The_Monkees#cite_note-rhino2012tour-101" style="counter-reset: mw-Ref 100;" id="mwBDY"><span class="mw-reflink-text" id="mwBDc">[100]</span></a></sup></li>
        <li id="mwBDg">A Midsummer's Night with the Monkees (Summer 2013) <small id="mwBDk">(Dolenz, Nesmith, Tork)</small></li>

        <li id="mwBDw">An Evening with the Monkees (2015) <small id="mwBD0">(Dolenz, Tork)</small></li>
        <li id="mwBD4">50th Anniversary Tour (2016) <small id="mwBD8">(Dolenz, Tork with selected appearances by Nesmith)</small></li>

        <li id="mwBEM">The Monkees Farewell Tour (Fall 2021)</li></ul>
